< user_id>
103514085620352453266< /user_id>
<Time>1443751246841<//Time>< text>
Though the weather outside was (slightly) frightful, the Dole Whip inside was so delightful!

My roommate's sister wanted to try this place when she was visiting, otherwise I might not have made the trip to the outskirts of the city.  It's worth it though.  The Dole Whip is just like what you get in Hawaii or at Disneyland, minus the long lines.  I got mine with pineapple chunks.  You can also get it with li hing powder, or go all out with guava and ice cream.  It was warm inside, and with the shakas all over, I was reminded of being back in the islands.

They also have rice plates and other edibles, along with shaved ice with lots of flavors to choose from.  I can imagine students nearby heading over to this place, because the prices are very reasonable.

The employees working there were friendly.  It was a welcoming atmosphere, and I'll have to make it out there sometime to try one of their rice plates.< /text>

<user_id>111727669481562056253< /user_id><Gmap_id>0x808e33d5e09d498d:0x94962ec7d54c749</Gmap_id>< Review>
Second time at a Loving Hut. The first time was in the Sunset in SF, which was great. We tried the hot dog (overpriced, tiny, and nothing special), the sesame bites (which were really soft and different from other sesame bites I have had, which normally mimic chicken rather than beef, in a sauce that was more gelatinous than sauce-ey), and, thankfully much better than the rest, the pesto grill (which was very good, would buy again).

I would probably not bring my non-vegan friends here for their first vegan restaurant, as the menu seems to be a hit or miss compared to other options in the area.<//Review>

<gmapID>0x808e33d5e09d498d:0x94962ec7d54c749< /gmapID><rating>4< /rating><Response>None<//Response>< text>
A vegan option at Oakridge Mall is very welcome, and I usually enjoy the "meatless" meats offered. I tried the Vermicelli Delicacy and Sesame Bites. The flavor of the Sesame Bites was unimpressive to me, I wouldn't get it again, but the Vermicelli I would get again.

The food quality here is just average in comparison to its non-vegan versions, as well as other vegan eateries I've tried. If the prices reflected the quality of food more I would give them 4 stars, but at $5 for an appetizer, and about $9 for some very average vegan dishes, I feel like its a bit too expensive.

But I still like the Loving Hut and will be back! I intend to try some of the other items which I see are more popular.</text>

<Review>Nuh-uh. Not this Starbucks. I'm sorry, but just, NOPE.

I was so excited when it first opened up. The other Starbucks was half hour walk away. When you have no car to drive, and when you love Starbucks as much as me, you'll understand how excited I was.

However, the drinks were just awful! Maybe it's because the staffs are all new? First, they gave me extra ice when I asked for light ice. I asked them to change it, but they just scooped out all the ice, and left the rest of the cup empty. They offered an explanation before I could point out the empty space. "Sorry, if I add more milk, it'll taste bad." Okay, fine, I'll just drink my half cup of mocha when I payed for the price of one.

Few days later, a friend asked me to bring her a cup of latte macchiato. I also got myself a cup of the mango dragonfruit drink. When she got her drink, it just tasted like heavy creamer and milk. There was absolutely no flavor in it other wise. Sadly, we had to throw the whole cup away. I drank my mango dragonfruit, but it was very watered down, and I think they forgot about the mango syrup...

Few months later (a week or two weeks ago), I thought they had enough time to learn, so I went and visited again. I got myself a cup of white chocolate mocha. Ugh... It looked just like milk (yes, pain white), and taste just like milk.... I asked the server about it, and she kindly remade my drink. "With extra pump of white mocha," she says. Only, this time it was so sweet, the mocha and chocolate flavor was way too much. Well, it's better than the milk...

It's going to be another few months before I come back. Hopefully, they'll be real Starbucks by then... Hopefully...<//Review><rating>3<//rating><gmapID>0x80c2dbb3c6734005:0x8afadd285820cadf<//gmapID>< userid>

<Text>Talk about being instant fans of a restaurant! We stopped by Benny's on our recent trip to Los Angeles and WOW, what a treat! This is a hole in the wall place with decent parking available. They do have a few tables inside and some outdoor seating too.

When we got there, they were working on a LARGE takeout order, but that did not impede them getting to our order on time :)

We ordered a few dishes and all of the dishes were really good! Quantity was decent too and the family enjoyed our meal here. So much so that we were back again for more of their good stuff!

Huevos Rancheros
Breakfast Quesadilla
Breakfast Burrito
Guacamole and Chips

Service was very friendly and efficient too. The shrimp wrap tasted perfect. It was really delicious!

< text>
We've been here a few times and the food is pretty hit or miss, depending on the menu item. The food is either terrible or great.

The burritos are flavorless and soggy. Additionally, the nachos are an absolute disaster. The nachos do not use a queso sauce as the menu description states. The nachos are just a huge wad of cheese and meat. There are minimal chips and the whole thing was an absolutely soggy mess. We ended up throwing out most of the nachos.

Conversely, we have had the tacos and quesadillas, which were much better. Both are large and pack a lot of flavor. The real bright spot here are the chirps, which are some of the best I've ever had.</text>

< Text>
First time here tonight and it was just alright. We started with the nacho plate to share and it was a huge disappointment. It was basically a sloppy, wet, mess. The chips were soggy and it wasn‚Äôt evenly prepared. You had a pound of guacamole that felt like thick sludge on half, tomatoes chopped on the other half with a light sprinkle of sour cream, pinto beans in between and cheese somewhere tbd. The dish didn‚Äôt have much flavor. I‚Äôm glad I didn‚Äôt judge the restaurant solely on that dish. We then had the taco plate and the steak was cooked perfectly (a little too much onion for my liking but I know for next time) and the ground beef and hard shell taco was my fav. Awesome flavor! The rice was great, beans were ok too. I wish the dish came with a side of sour cream. My husband tried a rotisserie chicken taco and that was pretty dried out. I am surprised considering rotisserie is their specialty!<//Text>

<Rating>4< /Rating>< text>
As a casual Mexican food spot, you can't get much better than Benny's in the Fox Hills/Westchester area. You order at the counter, they take your food fresh to order to eat on their patio or take to go. It can take a little while to get your food, but it's worth it to get some fresh and delicious Mexican food.

From burritos to nachos, tacos and quesadillas, Benny's has all of your favorites along with a basic salsa bar. The tortillas that they use on their burritos are really exceptional and set them apart from other Mexican joints in the area.

It's great food at a fair price. Benny's is our go-to for fast Mexican food that isn't Taco Bell in the area.< /text>

<Review>Don't let this tiny hole in wall fool you. The tacos here are not only affordable, they are also big on flavor!

I found this taco joint via Yelp when I visited LA in January. I was looking for something close to hotel and this was only couple of blocks away. You see, I grew up in LA and there's no shortage of taco places around. What makes Benny's different from others is that they also specialize in chicken rotisserie. And that's one of the tacos I ordered together with the Carnitas and Al Pastor.

Now, let's talk about quality. The Carnitas was super moist and tasty and the achiote marinated pork from the Al Pastor was full of flavor. Surprisingly, the Rotisserie Chicken taco was also juicy and delicious. I know its just chicken but this was done right. Prices were reasonable too. Tacos started at $3.50 each and goes up to $4.25 for the shrimp.

For around $12, I had a satisfying lunch at Benny's. It's casual, people are nice and not stingy with the meat.<//Review><Pics>None</Pics><Resp>None</Resp>< Gmap_id>
0x80c2b0ea7a7e0265:0x9d0ce9405491604f</Gmap_id>
</record></dataset><record>
<resp>None< /resp><user_id>112855782495203319904< /user_id><name>K. Elizabeth Meyer< /name>< text>
Incredible! If you have not been here, go...today! The Rotisserie chicken is amazing and so are all the Mexican dishes. I'm working my way through the menu. Love the chicken enchiladas (made with the rotisserie chicken and their famous green sauce); all the tacos (carnitas, carne asada, fish (fried or grilled), and shrimp (to die for); love the nachos; love the loaded fries; the quesadillas are worth writing home about, too!  Go. Today. You can thank me later.< /text>

<Review>Im a taco connoisseur. So when this place was recommended, i drove the extra miles to experience the hype.
The location is great but could use more parking...Especially with the option to sit and eat. I love the outdoor patio area.
The Aqua fresca drinks are delicious. The condiments bar is a huge plus. Customer service was great and service was pretty fast.
Unfortunately, i was not as pleased with the tacos. I ordered 3 shrimp, 3 Carne Asada and 2 watermelon drinks. My charge was almost $30. With that alone, i just knew my experience was going to be amazing. It was nothing to write home about. The chipotle sauce for the shrimp tacos actually makes the taco. I will stick to my local street vendors.</Review>< pictures>
